<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin);

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [31:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[31] & in2[31]) ^ (in1[31] & sum_temp[31]) ^ (in2[31] & sum_temp[31]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

wire [31:0] sum_w;
wire cout_w;

adder_16 adder_16_0(sum_w[15:0], cout_w, in1[15:0], in2[15:0], cin);
adder_16 adder_16_1(sum_w[31:16], cout, in1[31:16], in2[31:16], cout_w);

assign sum = sum_w;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [31:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[31] & in2[31]) ^ (in1[31] & sum_temp[31]) ^ (in2[31] & sum_temp[31]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [32:0] sum_wire;
  assign sum = sum_wire[31:0];
  assign cout = sum_wire[32];

  assign sum_wire = {in1, in2} + cin;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [31:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[31] & in2[31]) ^ (in1[31] & sum_temp[31]) ^ (in2[31] & sum_temp[31]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [31:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[31] & in2[31]) ^ (in1[31] & sum_temp[31]) ^ (in2[31] & sum_temp[31]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

  adder_32_bit adder_32_bit_1(sum_internal[1], cout_internal, in1[1], in2[1], cout_internal);

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.

                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin);

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [31:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[31] & in2[31]) ^ (in1[31] & sum_temp[31]) ^ (in2[31] & sum_temp[31]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [31:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[31] & in2[31]) ^ (in1[31] & sum_temp[31]) ^ (in2[31] & sum_temp[31]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [32:0] sum_wire;
  assign sum = sum_wire[31:0];
  assign cout = sum_wire[32];

  assign sum_wire = {in1, in2} + cin;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [31:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[31] & in2[31]) ^ (in1[31] & sum_temp[31]) ^ (in2[31] & sum_temp[31]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [31:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[31] & in2[31]) ^ (in1[31] & sum_temp[31]) ^ (in2[31] & sum_temp[31]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.

                      output cout,

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.

                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [31:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[31] & in2[31]) ^ (in1[31] & sum_temp[31]) ^ (in2[31] & sum_temp[31]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule

<s> //Design a 32-bit adder.
//There are two 32 bit inputs (in1 and in2) and a single carry-in input bit, cin.
//The outputs are a 32 bit value, [31:0] sum, and a single carry-out output bit, cout.
//The module should utilize the inputs (in1 and in2) and the cin bit to obtain the output sum and cout values.
module adder_32(output [31:0] sum,
                      output cout,
                      input [31:0] in1, in2,
                      input cin); 

  wire [31:0] sum_temp;
  wire cout_temp;

  assign sum_temp = in1 + in2;
  assign cout_temp = cin ^ (in1[31] & in2[31]) ^ (in1[31] & sum_temp[31]) ^ (in2[31] & sum_temp[31]);

  assign sum = sum_temp;
  assign cout = cout_temp;

endmodule
